   śarīraṃ bodhasāro me mamatā yatra bhūyasī // NBs_52.7 //	SarIram boDasAraH me mamatA yatra BUyasI // NBH-_52.7 //
   prāṇo me bodhasāro'yaṃ mamatā yatra bhūyasī /	prANaH me boDasAraH-ayam mamatA yatra BUyasI /
   jīvo me bodhasāro'yaṃ yena jīvāmyahaṃ sadā // NBs_52.8 //	jIvaH me boDasAraH-ayam yena jIvAmi-aham sadA // NBH-_52.8 //
   īśvaro bodhasāro me yato muktiprado mama /	ISvaraH boDasAraH me yatas mukti-pradaH mama /
   bodhasāraḥ paraṃ brahma bodhasārātparaṃ nahi // NBs_52.9 //	boDasAraH param brahma boDa-sArAt-param na-hi // NBH-_52.9 //
